## <a name="remarks"></a><span data-ttu-id="2c012-1664">備註</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2c012-1664">Remarks</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="2c012-1665">**MS DFSR 連接** 類別是分散式檔案系統 (DFS) Replication service 支援的一部分。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2c012-1665">The **ms-DFSR-Connection** class is a part of the Distributed File System (DFS) Replication service support.</span></span>
